# Weekly Report NÂ°4 for RubbleScout Project
School year 2023-2024

## Project Overview
- **Title:** RubbleScout
- **Tagline:** "Navigating Chaos Saving Lives"
- **Student:** Lorenz CAZAUBON
- **Supervisor:** Pascal MASSON
- **Institution:** Ecole Polytechnique Universitaire de Nice Sophia-Antipolis, Robotics Specialty (Autonomous Systems)
- **Location:** 930 route des Colles, 06410 BIOT France

## Objective
The primary focus of this session was to make progress in the physical modeling and initial assembly aspects of the RubbleScout project.

## Activities Undertaken
1. **3D Modeling and Laser Cutting**
   - Developed a 3D model of specific components for the robot.
   - Utilized laser cutting on plywood for creating precise parts. This process was essential for ensuring components fit accurately with the aluminum chassis.
   ```stl
      solid STLB ATF 12.14.0.127 COLOR=                                                      
   ```

2. **Selection of Fasteners**
   - Decided on the types of screws and bolts needed for mounting the electronic boards beneath the aluminum chassis.

3. **Collaborative Brainstorming**
   - Engaged in productive discussions with fellow students regarding the layout and design of various parts.
   - Focused on the design of protective casings and potential assembly methods.

4. **Design Considerations**
   - Contemplated the best approaches for assembling the casings and internal components, balancing accessibility, protection, and space optimization within the robot's chassis.

## Reflections and Next Steps
- This session, while seemingly less hands-on, was vital for the project's development. 
- The groundwork laid for more informed and efficient assembly decisions in the future.
- Next steps involve finalizing the designs of the casings and beginning the assembly process.
